# Corpus Rosetta Sweep Ledger, 2026-05-31

## Purpose

This ledger is the execution surface for applying the seven Rosetta agents
across Magnum Opus one folder, subfolder, or paper at a time.

It does not replace the protocol. It records the live queue and the evidence
needed before a pass is allowed to claim create / stabilize / destroy.

Authority stack:

1. [`00_CORPUS_SWEEP_PROTOCOL.md`](00_CORPUS_SWEEP_PROTOCOL.md) — procedure.
2. [`00_MASTER_MANIFEST.md`](00_MASTER_MANIFEST.md) — agent deployment map.
3. [`../../09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_index.py`](../../09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_index.py) — read-only Rosetta index.
4. [`../../09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_annotate.py`](../../09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_annotate.py) — reviewed annotation audit/apply helper.
5. [`../../09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_propose.py`](../../09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_propose.py) — proposal-only annotation scaffold.

---

Root discipline remains: fresh doctrine, product, and research files should be
routed to their owner lane or raw intake before any Rosetta repair claims them.

## Current Motions

| Motion | Result |
|---|---|
| Create | This ledger creates the durable queue surface for the persistent corpus-wide Rosetta-agent objective. |
| Stabilize | Rosetta helper scripts now resolve the live `01_EMERGENTISM/` tree before falling back to legacy `EMERGENTISM_ORG/`. |
| Destroy | The old active assumption that Rosetta tooling should scan `EMERGENTISM_ORG/` is destroyed as live authority; it remains only as backward-compatible fallback. |

## Tier-A Foundation Receipt

After the script path repair:

```text
python3 01_EMERGENTISM/09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_index.py --tier-a --include-missing --format json
entry_count 76
missing_count 0
by_level {'L1': 10, 'L2': 7, 'L3': 18, 'L4': 5, 'L5': 18, 'L6': 10, 'L7': 8}
```

```text
python3 01_EMERGENTISM/09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_annotate.py list-tier-a
COUNT=76
```

```text
python3 01_EMERGENTISM/09_TOOLS/01_SCRIPTS/rosetta_annotate.py audit --tier-a
rosetta audit ok
```

Interpretation:

- The toolchain now sees the live Tier-A surface.
- Tier-A foundation is audit-clean.
- RA-001 through RA-007 are patched; the next recursive wave can select the next folder/paper beyond the foundation queue.

## Recursive Wave Order

This order preserves local authority and keeps the objective broad without
turning it into a blind rewrite.

| Wave | Scope | Entry condition | Exit evidence |
|---|---|---|---|
| 0 | Toolchain and ledger | Helpers must see the live tree. | `rosetta_index.py --tier-a` returns nonzero entries and this ledger exists. |
| 1 | Tier-A foundation papers and route cards | RA-001 through RA-007 are queued. | `rosetta_annotate.py audit --tier-a` returns `rosetta audit ok`. |
| 2 | `01_EMERGENTISM` folders and subfolders | Each owner route has `AGENTS.md` / `README.md` where needed. | Folder-level ledger rows with create / stabilize / destroy and path-scoped commits. |
| 3 | Definitive book manuscript papers | Manuscript file is treated as paper, not bulk prose blob. | One ledger row per manuscript paper or chapter cluster. |
| 4 | `02_SKYZAI/02_AIA` medium layer | Engine/content split and AIA route cards are stable. | AIA route-card audit and app/scaffold separation preserved. |
| 5 | `03_VENTURES` | Entity owner route is read before edits. | Entity-specific sweep ledgers or route-card receipts. |
| 6 | `03_VENTURES/_PORTFOLIO` | Portfolio owner route is read before edits. | OFN/Tokencen/QNTM lane receipts; legal/finance claims tiered. |
| 7 | `02_SKYZAI/06_SPECTRE` and `02_SKYZAI/08_EVOLUTIONARY_NETWORK` | Small lanes after larger owner routes are stable. | Manifest-safe route-card receipts. |
| 8 | `90_ARCHIVE` | Active lanes no longer depend on ghost routes. | Archive-first K3 receipts; no silent deletion. |

---

## Ledger Row Template

Use this exact row shape for future passes:

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| Target | `<path>` |
| Unit type | folder / subfolder / paper |
| L1 perceive | `<broken, stale, duplicate, unsafe, falsely routed>` |
| L2 explore | `<candidate repairs>` |
| L3 audit | `<ranked repair and evidence tier>` |
| L4 execute | `<smallest patch>` |
| L5 stabilize | `<index, route, manifest, map>` |
| L6 destroy | `<pruned, demoted, archived, bounded, or no-op>` |
| L7 witness | `<compression note>` |
| Validators | `<commands and result>` |
| Commit | `<hash or pending>` |
| Residual risk | `<known dirty paths, follow-up, or none>` |

---

## Dirty-Checkout Guard

This ledger was created in a shared checkout with unrelated dirty work in root,
book manuscript files, `02_SKYZAI/02_AIA`, Aureus, Skyzai, and untracked research intake
files. Future passes must:

1. run `git status --short` first;
2. path-scope diffs and validators;
3. stage only the selected sweep unit;
4. verify `git diff --check HEAD^ HEAD` after commit;
5. keep unrelated dirty paths outside the Rosetta pass claim.

## Execution Surface

- **Canonical Path:** `01_EMERGENTISM/08_FRAMEWORK_SUPPORT/08_AGENTS/CORPUS_ROSETTA_SWEEP_LEDGER_2026_05_31.md`
